### The Alberto Rivera Controversy: Claims About Vatican Creating Islam

**Who Was Alberto Rivera?**

**Dr. Alberto Magno Romero Rivera** (1935-1997):
- Claimed to be **former Jesuit priest**
- Published by **Chick Publications** (1979-1988)
- **Alleged**: Vatican created Islam in 7th century to conquer Jerusalem and destroy true Christianity

**Rivera's Claims:**

According to Rivera's testimonies and comic books:

1. **Vatican created Islam** (7th century)
2. **Muhammad was trained by Catholic monk** named Bahira/Waraqa
3. **Purpose**: Use Muslim armies to destroy Orthodox Christians and Jews
4. **Goal**: Recapture Jerusalem for Rome
5. **Evidence**: Jesuit archives he allegedly saw while in the Order

**Assessment of Rivera's Claims:**

**Problems with Rivera's Account:**

**1. Anachronistic Timeline:**

- Islam arose **622-632 CE** (Muhammad's ministry)
- **Papal supremacy** not established until **538 CE** (marginally before), but papal power over distant regions was minimal
- **Jesuits founded 1540** (900+ years after Islam)
- **How could Jesuits** (1540) create Islam (622)? **Impossible.**

**2. Lack of Corroborating Evidence:**

- **No historical records** of Catholic monk "Bahira" training Muhammad in the way Rivera described
- **Islamic sources** mention Christian monk Bahira meeting young Muhammad, but **as recognizing him as prophet**, not training him
- **No Jesuit archives** contain Rivera's claimed documents (researchers checked)

**3. Catholic Church Officials Deny Rivera Was Priest:**

- **Diocese of San Juan** (Puerto Rico) stated **no record** of Rivera's ordination
- **Jesuits** deny Rivera was member
- **No verifiable documentation** of his claimed Jesuit education/ordination

**4. Credibility Issues:**

- Rivera made **multiple contradictory statements** about his background
- **Changed details** of story over time
- Associates reported Rivera had **credibility problems**

**Sources Critiquing Rivera:**
- Gary Metz, "Alberto: The Truth About His Story" (Cornerstone Magazine, 1981)
- Christianity Today investigations (1981)
- Catholic Diocese of San Juan records check

**However: Kernel of Historical Truth**

While Rivera's **specific claim** (Vatican created Islam) is **not historically supportable**, there **are documented connections** between early Catholic presence and early Islamic development:

**Documented Facts:**

**1. Christian Monk Bahira (Historical Figure):**

**Islamic sources** (Hadith, Ibn Ishaq's "Sirat Rasul Allah") mention:
- Christian monk named **Bahira** (or Sergius, or Nestorius in some accounts)
- Met young Muhammad (age 9 or 12) during caravan journey to Syria
- **Recognized signs** of prophethood in Muhammad
- Some accounts: Monk had conversations with Muhammad

**Historical Context:**
- Syria in 6th-7th century had **Nestorian Christians** (deemed heretics by Rome)
- Nestorians **rejected Trinity as Rome defined it**
- **Possible influence** on Islamic strict monotheism (Tawhid)

**Source:** Ibn Ishaq's "Sirat Rasul Allah" (earliest biography of Muhammad, translated by Alfred Guillaume, Oxford University Press, 1955)

**2. Khadija's Cousin Waraqa ibn Nawfal:**

**Islamic sources confirm:**
- Muhammad's first wife **Khadija** had cousin named **Waraqa ibn Nawfal**
- Waraqa was **Christian convert** (possibly Nestorian or Ebionite Christian)
- **Affirmed Muhammad's prophethood** when Muhammad first received revelations
- Told Muhammad he was like Moses and would be prophet

**Significance:**
- **Christian influence** confirmed in early Islamic development
- But **not evidence of Vatican conspiracy** (Waraqa was Eastern Christian, likely opposed to Rome)

**Source:** Sahih al-Bukhari (most authoritative Hadith collection), Book 1, Hadith 3

**3. Early Islamic Expansion Benefited Rome Strategically:**

**Objective Fact:**
- Islamic conquests (638-711 CE) **destroyed Byzantine (Orthodox Christian) power** in Middle East, North Africa, Spain
- **Vatican's Christian rival** eliminated by Muslim armies
- Rome emerged as **dominant Christian center** in West

**This doesn't prove Vatican created Islam**, but shows **Vatican benefited** from Islamic expansion

### "Follow the Money" - Proof That All Roads Lead to Rome

**The Ancient Saying: "All roads lead to Rome"**

**Historical Context:**

- **Roman Empire** built roads radiating from Rome to all provinces
- **Purpose**: Control, taxation, military movement, commerce
- **Saying became metaphor**: "Everything eventually connects back to Rome"

**Modern Reality: Still True**

**Today, if you "follow the money," you will discover that ALL global financial power ultimately flows through or connects back to Rome (the Vatican).**

#### The Vatican Banking Network: Hub of Global Finance

**Institute for Religious Works (IOR)**

**Actual Purpose**:

### The European Sunday Law Legislative Record: Brussels as the Proving Ground

**The European Union has been the primary testing ground for Vatican-backed Sunday rest legislation since the 1990s. This is not coincidence — the same Catholic lobbying architecture that operates at the UN (COMECE, the European Sunday Alliance, Caritas Europa) operates at the heart of Brussels. Each EU legislative cycle pushes Sunday normalization one step further. What fails this decade is reintroduced the next — refined, re-packaged, and advanced.**

---

#### 1. EU Working Time Directive (Directive 93/104/EC, 1993) — The First Attempt

**Background:**
In November 1993 the European Council adopted the **Working Time Directive (93/104/EC)**, establishing minimum rest periods for workers across all EU member states. Article 5 of the original draft included the following explicit clause:

> *"The minimum rest period referred to in paragraph 1 shall in principle include Sunday."*

**The Significance:**
This was the first time a major supranational legislative body attempted to codify **Sunday by name** as the standard weekly rest day across an entire continent — affecting every employer, every employee, in every EU member state.

**Opposition and Court Battle:**
The United Kingdom (under the Conservative government of John Major) challenged the directive at the **European Court of Justice**, arguing it exceeded the EU's competence on health-and-safety grounds.

- **ECJ Ruling — Joined Cases C-84/94 (United Kingdom v. Council of the EU, 1996)**: The Court upheld most of the directive but **struck down Article 5's Sunday-specific requirement**, ruling it had not been adequately justified as a health measure.
- The Court did **not** rule Sunday rest was wrong in principle — only that the Sunday specification lacked sufficient scientific/health justification.

**Result:** Sunday removed from the final text. But the principle was established: the EU framework could, in theory, mandate Sunday rest — it simply needed better legal justification.

**Catholic Lobbying Response:**
COMECE (Commission of the Bishops' Conferences of the European Community) immediately began lobbying for a revised directive that would reintroduce Sunday as the default rest day under health, social, and environmental rationales.

---

#### 2. European Parliament Resolutions on Sunday Rest (1988–2017)

The European Parliament has passed **multiple non-binding resolutions** identifying Sunday as the preferred weekly rest day:

| Year | Resolution / Document | Key Language |
|------|----------------------|--------------|
| **1988** | EP Resolution on the Working Week | Recognized Sunday as "traditional" rest day; called on member states to protect it |
| **1993** | Working Time Directive debate | EP supported Sunday clause (defeated in Article 5 by ECJ) |
| **2009** | Estrela Report (Work-Life Balance) | Called Sunday "socially necessary" as common rest day; passed EP plenary |
| **2017** | Work-Life Balance Directive proposal | Sunday identified as preferred family rest day in EP committee amendments |
| **2023** | Platform Work Directive debate | Sunday rest provisions included in Committee on Employment drafts |

**Key Pattern:** Every 5–8 years a new EP report, directive, or amendment cycle revives the Sunday rest question. Each cycle the language grows stronger and the opposition weaker.

---

#### 3. The Estrela Report (2009) — The Clearest Sunday Push

**European Parliament Report A6-0241/2009** — commonly called the **Estrela Report** after Portuguese MEP Edite Estrela — was the most explicit European Sunday push since 1993.

**What It Said:**
- Identified **Sunday as the socially necessary common weekly rest day** for family cohesion and worker wellbeing
- Recommended member states legislate Sunday as the default day off — not just "one day in seven"
- Cited health studies, family research, and — critically — **COMECE submissions** as supporting evidence

**Voting Outcome:**
The report passed the **European Parliament plenary** on 11 March 2009, by 423 votes to 196.

**Significance:**
- A majority of elected EU representatives voted **in favour** of identifying Sunday as the normative rest day
- The vote was non-binding on member states — but it established political consensus
- COMECE celebrated the vote publicly as a "significant step" toward Sunday recognition in EU law

---

#### 4. COMECE — The Vatican's Official Brussels Lobbying Machine

**Full Name:** Commission of the Bishops' Conferences of the European Community  
**Founded:** 1980  
**Headquarters:** Rue Joseph II, Brussels — two blocks from the European Commission

**What COMECE Does:**
COMECE is the **official institutional voice of the Catholic Church** at the European Union. It is not a fringe lobby group — it has:
- Permanent accreditation with the European Commission, Parliament, and Council
- Regular formal dialogue sessions with EU leadership (mandated under **Article 17 of the Treaty on the Functioning of the EU**)
- Staff of policy experts who monitor and submit position papers on every major EU directive

**Funding:**
COMECE is substantially funded through the **German Kirchensteuer** (Church tax) system — the same concordat-based revenue stream detailed in the Concordats section above. Germany's Catholic bishops pay a significant portion of COMECE's Brussels operational budget.

**Sunday Rest Lobbying Record:**
- Submitted formal briefs in support of Sunday language in the **1993 Working Time Directive**
- Lobbied actively for the **2009 Estrela Report** Sunday provisions
- Published **"Sunday: European Day of Rest"** position paper (2012) calling for legally protected Sunday rest across the EU
- Submitted to the European Commission consultation on **Work-Life Balance Directive (2017)** explicitly requesting Sunday as default rest day
- Partners with the **European Sunday Alliance** (see below) to coordinate multi-denominational lobbying pressure

**COMECE's Own Words (2012 Position Paper):**
> *"Sunday as a common day of rest and family life is a shared European value across religious and cultural traditions. The European Union should give legal recognition to this value through binding legislation."*

---

#### 5. The European Sunday Alliance — A Broader Coalition

**Founded:** 2011  
**Members:** 100+ organizations across EU member states  
**Composition:** Catholic bishops' conferences, Protestant church federations, trade unions, family associations, and social welfare groups

**Purpose:** The European Sunday Alliance was created specifically to build a **broader-than-Catholic** coalition for Sunday rest legislation — deliberately recruiting secular trade unions and family groups to argue Sunday rest on *social* rather than *religious* grounds, thereby bypassing religious-liberty objections.

**Prophetic Significance:**
This is exactly the strategy described in Revelation 13:12 — the second beast "causes the earth and them that dwell therein to worship the first beast" by marshalling all economic, social, and governmental forces. The European Sunday Alliance does not frame Sunday as "worship" — it frames it as "social necessity," "family time," and "environmental healing." The religious content is hidden; the coercion mechanism is secular.

**Key Activities:**
- Annual **European Sunday Summit** in Brussels (joint Catholic-Protestant-trade union conference)
- **"1in7" Campaign** — arguing statistically that removing Sunday rest harms mental health, family stability, and social cohesion
- Commissioned **Economic Research**: Prognos AG (2012) study claiming Sunday trading costs societies more than it gains — funded by Sunday Alliance, cited in EP debates

---

#### 6. Work-Life Balance Directive (2019) — Sunday Rest Embedded in EU Law

**Directive 2019/1158/EU** on Work-Life Balance for parents and carers became binding EU law on 2 August 2022.

While it does not name Sunday explicitly, its provisions on **parental leave, flexible working arrangements, and family time requirements** were drafted with COMECE and European Sunday Alliance input, and embed the principle that a **common family rest day** is a legitimate legislative objective.

This is the **legislative beachhead**: once the EU accepts that it may regulate which day families rest, the specific day (Sunday) can be inserted by amendment in a future revision cycle.

---

#### 7. Current EU Legislative Environment (2024–2026)

**Active in the European Parliament:**
- **Platform Work Directive** (2024) — Sunday rest provisions in committee amendments
- **AI Regulation implementation** — monitoring of work patterns could make Sunday compliance trackable
- **Green Deal / Right to Repair / Circular Economy Framework** — "sustainable consumption" arguments being used to justify reduced Sunday commerce

**European Commission:**
- **Commissioner for Jobs and Social Rights** portfolio explicitly includes "work-life balance" and "European Social Pillar" — Sunday rest falls within this mandate
- **Article 31 of the EU Charter of Fundamental Rights**: *"Every worker has the right to... a weekly rest period."* COMECE has submitted legal opinions that this Article implies Sunday by historical and cultural context.

**The Direction of Travel:**
Each legislative cycle moves in one direction only. The 1993 directive was defeated on Sunday — but it established the legal framework. The 2009 EP resolution established political consensus. The 2019 directive embedded the family-day principle. The 2024–2026 cycle will introduce the next increment.

---

#### 8. The Vatican–EU–UN Triangle: A Coordinated System

The EU Sunday legislative push does not operate in isolation. It is coordinated with:

| Level | Institution | Mechanism |
|-------|-------------|-----------|
| **Global** | United Nations | ILO conventions on rest; Laudato Si' climate framework |
| **Regional** | European Union | Working Time Directive; Work-Life Balance Directive; Article 17 church dialogue |
| **National** | Member States | Concordats (Germany, Italy, Spain, Poland); national Sunday trading laws |
| **Local** | Bishops' Conferences | COMECE; National implementation pressure |

**The Pope Addresses the EU Parliament Directly:**
- **Pope John Paul II addressed the European Parliament** in 1988: urged Sunday protection
- **Pope Francis sent a formal message** to EU leaders in 2017 (Rome Declaration anniversary): called for a Europe rooted in its "Christian roots" — code language well understood by Catholic MEPs

**Prophetic Summary:**
Revelation 17:12-13 describes "ten kings" who "receive power as kings one hour with the beast" and give "their power and strength unto the beast." The EU — as a confederation of 27 sovereign nations that have pooled legislative authority — is the clearest modern archetype of this structure. It is prophecy being fulfilled in slow motion.**
